First two terms:
- Term 1: `0.1387*(P/8.038 - 1)*(1 - P/70.018)*P` — this is a cubic in P
- Term 2: `0.1387*(1 - P/70.018)*P` — this is quadratic in P
- Term 3: `0.1387*P/(1 + exp(-8.038*(P - 0.5894)))` — this is a sigmoid-weighted term in P

The GT is purely a function of P (no t dependence). So any candidate must allow all t-dependent terms to vanish (by setting their constants to 0).

Let me look for candidates that, after setting t-terms to zero, can produce: a cubic polynomial in P plus a sigmoid-type term in P.

**Candidate 4:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(P+c3) + Pc4*exp(Pc5) + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`

Setting c6=0 removes t-dependence. We get: `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(P+c3) + Pc4*exp(Pc5)`. The sigmoid `P/(1+exp(-a(P-b)))` is not the same as `P*exp(cP)`. Not a match.

**Candidate 11:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*exp(Pc3 + c4) + c5*t*exp(c6*t)`

Setting c5=0: `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*exp(Pc3 + c4)`. This gives polynomial + P*exp(linear in P), but GT has P/(1+exp(...)), not P*exp(...). Not equivalent.

**Candidate 29:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*log(Pc3+1) + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(c7*exp(Pc8 + c9*t)+1)`

Setting c4=0, c9=0: `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*log(Pc3+1) + c6*log(c7*exp(Pc8)+1)`

Note that `log(c7*exp(Pc8)+1) = log(exp(Pc8)*(c7 + exp(-Pc8))) = Pc8 + log(c7 + exp(-Pc8))`. 

If c7=1: `log(1+exp(Pc8))`. This is the softplus function. The derivative of softplus is the sigmoid, but softplus itself isn't P*sigmoid.

The GT's sigmoid term is `0.1387*P/(1+exp(-8.038(P-0.5894)))`. This isn't expressible as polynomials + log terms.

**Candidate 24:** `Pc0 + Pc1*exp(Pc2) + c3*exp(Pc4) + c5`

No t-dependence. We have: `Pc0 + Pc1*exp(Pc2) + c3*exp(Pc4) + c5`. The GT has cubic terms (P³) which can't come from these exponential forms. Not a match.

**Candidate 26:** `P³c0/(P+c1) + P²c2/(P+c1) + Pc3/(P+c1) + Pc4*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1) + Pc7*exp(Pc8) + c9*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1)`

The rational part `(P³c0 + P²c2 + Pc3)/(P+c1)` can produce a quadratic + constant + correction term. The `P*exp(cP)` term doesn't match P*sigmoid. Not equivalent.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.13870625668024555*(-1 + P/8.038138014396704)*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*P/(1 + exp(-8.038138014396704*(-0.5894251550796137 + P)))
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.13870625668024555, a = 8.038138014396704, b = 70.01799944958296, d = 0.5894251550796137.

**Term 1:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 2:** α*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 3:** α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(-d + P)))

Let me expand Terms 1 and 2:

Term 1: α*P*(P/a - 1)*(1 - P/b) = α*P*[(P/a - 1) - (P/a - 1)*P/b]
= α*P*[P/a - 1 - P²/(ab) + P/b]

Term 2: α*P*(1 - P/b) = α*P - α*P²/b

Combined Terms 1+2:
= α*P*[P/a - 1 - P²/(ab) + P/b] + α*P - α*P²/b
= α*[P²/a - P - P³/(ab) + P²/b + P - P²/b]
= α*[P²/a - P³/(ab)]
= α*P²/a*(1 - P/b)
= α*P²/a - α*P³/(ab)

So GT = α*P²/a - α*P³/(ab) + α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P - d)))

Numerically:
- α/a = 0.13870625668024555/8.038138014396704 ≈ 0.01725
- α/(ab) = 0.01725/70.018 ≈ 0.000246
- The sigmoid term: α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d)))

So GT = c₁*P² + c₂*P³ + c₃*P*sigmoid(c₄*(P - c₅))

where sigmoid(x) = 1/(1+exp(-x)).

**Key structural features of GT:**
1. A polynomial in P: terms P² and P³
2. A sigmoid-like term in P: P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d)))
3. **NO dependence on t** — the GT is independent of t!

This is crucial. Any candidate with t-dependence must have those t-terms zeroed out.

Now let me check each candidate. For candidates with t-dependence, I need to verify that t-terms can be set to zero AND the remaining P-terms can match the GT structure.

The GT has three basis function types in P:
- P² (polynomial)
- P³ (polynomial)
- P*sigmoid(linear in P) = P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d)))

Let me go through each candidate:

### Candidate 1:
`P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3 + c4*tanh(c5*t + c6) + c7*t/(c8 + t**2)`

Set c4=0, c7=0 to kill t-terms. Remaining: c0*P³ + (c1+c2)*P² + c3*P.
This is a cubic polynomial in P. GT has a sigmoid term, not just polynomial. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + P**c4*c5*log(P*c6 + 1) + c7*t + c8`

Set c7=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + P^c4*c5*log(P*c6+1) + c8.
Has log terms, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3 + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Set c4=0. Remaining: (c0+c1)*P² + (c2+c3)*P + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8+1)+c9).
Has sin(log(...)) term, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2/(P + c3) + P*c4*exp(P*c5) + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`

Set c6=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2/(P+c3) + P*c4*exp(P*c5).
P*c2/(P+c3) = c2*P/(P+c3) — this is a rational function, not sigmoid.
P*c4*exp(P*c5) — exponential, not sigmoid.
Neither of these can produce P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))). **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4*exp(P*c5) + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`

Set c6=0, c3=0 (making exp(c3*t)=1). Remaining: P²*c0 + (c1+c2)*P + P*c4*exp(P*c5).
P*exp(P*c5) is not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6:
`P**3*c0/(c1 + t**2) + P**2*c2/(c1 + t**2) + P*c3/(c1 + t**2) + P*c4*t**2/(c1 + t**2) + c5/(c1 + t**2) + c6*t/(c1 + t**2) + c7*t**2/(c1 + t**2)`

Factor out 1/(c1+t²): everything is divided by (c1+t²). This can't be made t-independent unless c1→∞ which would zero everything, or we look at it differently. If c1=0, we get 1/t² times stuff, still t-dependent. **NO MATCH.**

Wait, actually if c1 is very large... no, we need exact equivalence. Let me reconsider. We can set c6=0 to kill the odd t term. Then:
= [P³*c0 + P²*c2 + P*c3 + c5]/(c1+t²) + [P*c4 + c7]*t²/(c1+t²)

For t-independence, we need the t²-dependent parts to combine properly. Note that 1/(c1+t²) + t²/(c1+t²) = (c1+t²)/(c1+t²) = 1 when c1 is the same. So:
= P³*c0/(c1+t²) + P²*c2/(c1+t²) + P*(c3/(c1+t²) + c4*t²/(c1+t²)) + c5/(c1+t²) + c7*t²/(c1+t²)

For P term: c3/(c1+t²) + c4*t²/(c1+t²) = (c3 + c4*t²)/(c1+t²). For t-independence, need c4 = c3/c1, giving c3*(1+t²/c1)/(c1+t²) = c3/c1. Wait, that requires c4*c1 = c3, giving (c3+c4*t²)/(c1+t²) = c4*(c1+t²)/(c1+t²) = c4 only if c3 = c4*c1.

Similarly for constant: (c5+c7*t²)/(c1+t²) = c7 if c5 = c7*c1.

And P³*c0/(c1+t²) and P²*c2/(c1+t²) are still t-dependent unless c0=0 and c2=0.

If c0=0, c2=0: remaining is c4*P + c7. Just linear in P. Can't match GT. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*tanh(c5*t + c6) + c7*exp(P**c8*c9)`

Set c3=0, c4=0 (or c5=0 and absorb tanh(c6) into constant). With c3=0: P²*c0 + (c1+c2)*P + c4*tanh(c5*t+c6) + c7*exp(c9*P^c8).

Set c4=0 or c5=0. If c5=0: c4*tanh(c6) is a constant.
Remaining: P²*c0 + (c1+c2)*P + const + c7*exp(c9*P^c8).

exp(c9*P^c8) is not a sigmoid function. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 8:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P*c4*log(P*c5 + 1) + c6*log(c7*t + 1)`

Set c6=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P*c4*log(P*c5+1).
Has exp and log terms, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 9:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2/(P*c3 + 1)**2 + c4*t + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Set c4=0. Has sin(log(...)) and rational terms, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + P**c4*c5 + c6*t + c7 + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

Set c6=0, c8=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c5*P^c4 + c7.
Has log and power-law terms, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 11:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3 + c4) + c5*t*exp(c6*t)`

Set c5=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c4)*exp(P*c3).
= P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*C*exp(P*c3) where C = c2*exp(c4).

P*exp(P*c3) is not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 12:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1/(P + c2) + P*c3 + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6`

Set c4=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P²*c1/(P+c2) + P*c3 + c6.
P²*c1/(P+c2) is a rational function. Let me expand: P²/(P+c2) = P - c2 + c2²/(P+c2).
So: P²*c0 + c1*P - c1*c2 + c1*c2²/(P+c2) + P*c3 + c6
= c0*P² + (c1+c3)*P + c1*c2²/(P+c2) + (c6-c1*c2)

This gives polynomial + rational term c1*c2²/(P+c2). This is not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 13:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + P**c4*c5 + c6*tanh(c7*t + c8) + c9`

Set c6=0 (or c7=0). Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c5*P^c4 + const.
Has log and power-law, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14:
Similar structure to Candidate 6 with t² terms. Let me check if t-dependence can be eliminated.

`P**3*c0/(c1+t²) + P**2*c2*t²/(c1+t²) + P**2*c3/(c1+t²) + P**2*c4/(c1+t²) + P**2*c5*t²/(c1+t²) + P*c6/(c1+t²) + P*c7*t²/(c1+t²) + c8*t/(c1+t²)`

Set c8=0. Group by powers of P:
- P³: c0/(c1+t²) — t-dependent unless c0=0
- P²: (c2*t² + c3 + c4 + c5*t²)/(c1+t²) = ((c2+c5)*t² + c3+c4)/(c1+t²). For t-independence: (c2+c5) = (c3+c4)/c1, giving constant = (c3+c4)/c1 = (c2+c5).
- P: (c6 + c7*t²)/(c1+t²). For t-independence: c7 = c6/c1.

But P³ term requires c0=0. Then we only have P² and P terms (polynomial). Can't match sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 15:
`P**3*c0/(P+c1) + P**2*c2/(P+c1) + P*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1) + P*c7/(P+c8) + c9*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1)`

Set c5=0 to make tanh constant: tanh(c6) = const K.
= P³*c0/(P+c1) + P²*c2/(P+c1) + P*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4*K/(P+c1) + P*c7/(P+c8) + c9*K/(P+c1)

Combine: [P³*c0 + P²*c2 + P*(c3+c4*K) + c9*K]/(P+c1) + P*c7/(P+c8)

The first fraction: P³*c0/(P+c1) = c0*P² - c0*c1*P + c0*c1² - c0*c1³/(P+c1) (polynomial long division).

Actually, let me do this more carefully. P³/(P+c1) = P² - c1*P + c1² - c1³/(P+c1).

So the first part becomes a polynomial plus rational terms with denominator (P+c1), and the second part has denominator (P+c8).

This gives polynomial + rational functions, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 16:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1/(P**2 + c2) + P*c3 + P**c4*c5 + c6*t + c7 + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

Set c6=0, c8=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P²*c1/(P²+c2) + P*c3 + c5*P^c4 + c7.
Has rational and power-law terms, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 17:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3 + P*c4*exp(c2*t) + P*c5*log(P*c6 + 1) + c7*t/(c8 + t**2) + c9`

Set c2=0, c7=0. Then: P²*(c0+c1) + P*(c3+c4) + P*c5*log(P*c6+1) + c9.
Has log term, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 18:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*log(P**2*c5 + c6*t + 1)`

Set c2=0, c6=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + c4*log(P²*c5+1).
Has log(P²+const), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 19:
`P**3*c0/(P+c1) + P**2*c2/(P+c1) + P*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1) + c7*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1)`

Set c5=0: tanh(c6) = K (constant).
= [P³*c0 + P²*c2 + P*(c3+c4*K) + c7*K]/(P+c1)

This is a cubic polynomial divided by (P+c1). By polynomial division:
= c0*P² + (c2-c0*c1)*P + (c3+c4*K - c1*(c2-c0*c1)) + [c7*K - c1*(c3+c4*K-c1*(c2-c0*c1))]/(P+c1)

This gives: quadratic polynomial + constant/(P+c1). Not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 20:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*t + c9))`

Set c4=0, c8=0: c6*exp(c7*sin(c9)) = constant.
Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + const.
Has log, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 21:
`P**3*c0/(P+c1) + P**2*c2/(P+c1) + P**2*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4/(P+c1) + P*c5/(P+c1) + P*c6*tanh(c7*t+c8)/(P+c1) + c9*tanh(c7*t+c8)/(P+c1)`

Set c7=0: tanh(c8) = K.
= [P³*c0 + P²*(c2+c3) + P*(c4+c5+c6*K) + c9*K]/(P+c1)

Same as Candidate 19 structure. Polynomial + const/(P+c1). Not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 21 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 22:
`P**2*c0 + c1*t*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(P*c6 + 1) + c7)`

Set c1=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(P*c6+1)+c7).
Has sin(log(...)), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 22 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 23:

Set c6=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c5*P^c4 + c8.
Has log and power-law, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 24:
`P*c0 + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + c3*exp(P*c4) + c5`

No t-dependence. P*c0 + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + c3*exp(P*c4) + c5.
Has P*exp(P*c) and exp(P*c) terms. These are exponential in P, not sigmoid or polynomial. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 24 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 25:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + c4*t/(c5 + t**2) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*log(P*c9 + 1)`

Set c4=0, c8=0 (or c7=0). If c8=0: c7*log(P*c9+1) is P-dependent.
Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c6 + c7*log(P*c9+1).
Has log terms, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

### Candidate 26:
`P**3*c0/(P+c1) + P**2*c2/(P+c1) + P*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1) + P*c7*exp(P*c8) + c9*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1)`

Set c5=0: tanh(c6)=K.
= [P³*c0 + P²*c2 + P*(c3+c4*K) + c9*K]/(P+c1) + P*c7*exp(P*c8)

The rational part gives polynomial + const/(P+c1). Plus P*exp(P*c8).
Not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Set c5=0: c4*tanh(c6) = const.
Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1*log(P*c2+1) + P*c3 + const + c7*exp(c8*sqrt(P)).
Has log and exp(sqrt(P)), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

### Candidate 28:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Set c4=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8+1)+c9).

### Candidate 29:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8 + c9*t) + 1)`

Set c4=0, c9=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1).

Now, c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1) = c6*log(c7) + c6*log(exp(P*c8) + 1/c7)... Hmm, let me think about this differently.

Actually, log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1). If c7 = 1, this is the softplus function: log(exp(P*c8)+1).

The softplus function log(1+exp(x)) has derivative sigmoid(x) = 1/(1+exp(-x)). But we need P*sigmoid, not softplus.

The GT has P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))). This is P*sigmoid(a*(P-d)).

log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1) is a softplus-like function, not P*sigmoid. These are different functions. **NO MATCH.**

Wait, but let me reconsider. Could P*c2*log(P*c3+1) somehow combine with the softplus? No, log(P*c3+1) and P*sigmoid are fundamentally different basis functions.

Candidate 29 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 30:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*log(P**2*c6 + c7*t + 1) + c8*t/(c9 + t**2)`

Set c2=0, c7=0, c8=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + c4 + c5*log(P²*c6+1).
Has log(P²+const), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Can't eliminate sqrt(c5+t²) without setting c4=0. Then: P²*c0 + P*c1*log(P*c2+1) + P*c3 + c6/P^5.
Has log and 1/P^5, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 32:
Complex expression with P^(1/4), P^(5/4), etc. These fractional powers can't match the GT which has integer powers and sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 32 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 33:

Just a quadratic polynomial. Missing P³ and sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

### Candidate 36:
`P**3*c0/(P+c1) + P**2*c2/(P+c1) + P*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1) + c7*tanh(c5*t+c6)/(P+c1) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

P*(P*c5+1)^c6 is a power-law expression, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

### Candidate 38:
`P**3*c0/(P+c1) + P**2*c2/(P+c1) + P**2*c3/(P+c1) + P*c4/(P+c1) + P*c5/(P+c1) + P*c6*t/(P+c1) + P*c7/(P+c1) + c8/(P+c1) + c9*t/(P+c1)`

= [P³*c0 + P²*(c2+c3) + P*(c4+c5+c7) + c8]/(P+c1)

### Candidate 39:

### Candidate 40:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + P**c4*c5 + c6*t + c7`

Set c6=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c5*P^c4 + c7.
Has log and power-law, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 40 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 41:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3 + 1) + c4*t/(c5 + t**2) + c6 + c7*log(c8*exp(c9*t) + 1)`

Set c4=0. For the last term, set c9=0: c7*log(c8+1) = constant.
Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c6 + const.
Has log(P+const), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 41 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 42:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*t/(c6 + t**2) + c7*exp(P**c8*c9)`

Set c2=0, c5=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + c4 + c7*exp(c9*P^c8).
Has exp(P^c), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 42 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 43:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P**c2*c3 + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8 + 1) + c9)`

Set c4=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P*c1 + c3*P^c2 + c6*sin(c7*log(P*c8+1)+c9).
Has power-law and sin(log(...)), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 43 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 44:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3 + P*c4/(P + c5) + c6*log(c7*t + 1)`

Set c2=0, c6=0. Remaining: P²*(c0+c1) + P*c3 + P*c4/(P+c5).
P*c4/(P+c5) = c4*P/(P+c5) = c4 - c4*c5/(P+c5).
So: (c0+c1)*P² + (c3+c4)*P - c4*c5/(P+c5) + ... wait, let me redo.
P*c4/(P+c5) = c4*P/(P+c5). This is rational, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 44 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 45:
`P**2*c0 + c1*t*exp(c2*t) + c3*sin(c4*log(P*c5 + 1) + c6) + c7*log(P*c8 + 1)`

Set c1=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + c3*sin(c4*log(P*c5+1)+c6) + c7*log(P*c8+1).
Has sin(log(...)) and log, not sigmoid. Missing P³ term and sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 45 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 46:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1*log(P*c2 + 1) + P*c3 + P*c4 + c5*t*exp(c6*t)`

Set c5=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P²*c1*log(P*c2+1) + P*(c3+c4).
Has P²*log(P+const), not sigmoid or P³. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 46 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 47:
`P**2*c0 + P*P**c1*c2 + P*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5/(P + c6) + c7*t**2 + c8*t + c9`

Set c7=0, c8=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + c2*P^(1+c1) + (c3+c4)*P + c5*P/(P+c6) + c9.

Hmm, P^(1+c1) with c1 free. If c1=2, we get P³. And c5*P/(P+c6) is rational.

But we need P*sigmoid, not P/(P+c6). The sigmoid is 1/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))), which is fundamentally different from 1/(P+c6). **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 47 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 48:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1/(P**2 + c2) + c3*t*exp(c4*t) + c5*sin(c6*log(P*c7 + 1) + c8)`

Set c3=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + P²*c1/(P²+c2) + c5*sin(c6*log(P*c7+1)+c8).
Has rational and sin(log(...)), not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 48 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 49:
`P**2*c0 + P**2*c1/(P**2 + c2) + P*c3 + P**c4*c5 + c6*tanh(c7*t + c8) + c9`

Set c7=0: c6*tanh(c8) = const.
Remaining: P²*c0 + P²*c1/(P²+c2) + P*c3 + c5*P^c4 + const.
Has rational and power-law, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 49 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 50:
`P**2*c0 + P*P**c1*c2 + P*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5*log(P*c6 + 1) + c7*t**2 + c8*t + c9`

Set c7=0, c8=0. Remaining: P²*c0 + c2*P^(1+c1) + (c3+c4)*P + P*c5*log(P*c6+1) + c9.
Has power-law and log, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 50 verdict: [NO MATCH]

## Summary

The GT contains a sigmoid function P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))), which is a very specific nonlinear function. None of the candidates contain a sigmoid (1/(1+exp(...))) or equivalent functional form. The candidates use log, sin, tanh, exp, rational functions, and power-law terms, none of which can exactly replicate a sigmoid function.

Note: tanh is related to sigmoid by tanh(x) = 2*sigmoid(2x) - 1, but in the GT the sigmoid multiplies P, creating P*sigmoid(f(P)), while candidates with tanh have tanh as a function of t (not P), so they can't match.
